ARIE 1929-1930 [vol. 052]


A. List of copper-plates examined during the year 1929-30.


ARIE/1929-1930/A/1929-30/1 (page 4)
Placement
The Trustee of the Sundara-rāja-Perumāḷ temple at Aḻagarkōyil, Madura taluk, Madura district.
Dynasty
Sētupati
King
Vijayaraghunātha-Sētupati-dēva.
Date
Śaka 1634, Nan-dana, Dakshiṇā-yana, Grīshma, Āshāḍha, ba. amāvāsyā. Tues-day, Pushya.
Language
Tamil
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
South-Indian Inscriptions.
Remarks
States that Muttuvayiravanāthadēva, son of Kaḍambattēvar who was the elder brother of the king and was residing at Uttarakōśamaṅgai, remitted half of the revenue from the villages Āykkuḍi and Śunda-ṉāvūr which belonged to Tiruveṅ-kaṭāchārya, son of Tirumalaiyāṇḍa-Tiruveṅkaṭāchārya, for the ex-penses of feeding in the temple of Aḻagar and for digging a tank between the temple and Appaṉ-Tirupati. The king calls him-self ‘the lord of Tēvainagar (Rāmēśvaram)’ and had the ‘Hanu-mān-banner’.
ARIE/1929-1930/A/1929-30/2 (page 4)
Placement
Mr. Dupati Papayya, Priest of the Śiva temple at Goṭṭi-mukkala. Palnad taluk, Guntur district.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1725, Rudhi-rōdgāri, Mārga, śu. 5, Sunday.
Language
Telugu
Origin
Do.
Edition
Do.
Remarks
Registers the varshāśana-patrikā given by the 102 nagaras of Goṭṭi-mukkala for the maintenance of worship and lamps in the temple of Uttarēśvarasvāmin at the village, and specifies the rates of tolls to be levied upon various articles of merchandise passing through the ghat (at that place).

B. Stone inscriptions copied during the year 1929-30.


GANJAM DISTRICT


CHICACOLE TALUK


ARIE/1929-1930/B/1929-30/1 (page 5)
Placement
Peddapadu.--On a slab lying in front of the Karnam's house.
Dynasty
Gajapati
King
Bhā[nudēva]
Date
Śaka 1287, 14th year, Karkaṭa, śu. 5.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Damaged. Seems to register grant of land for offerings to the god Sōmanãtha, by Nandanamahārāju. Mentions Mallinātha.
ARIE/1929-1930/B/1929-30/2 (page 5)
Placement
Ippili.--On a stone lying in a garden near the Karnam's house.
Dynasty
Eastern Gaṅga.
King
Chō[ḍa]gaṅgadēva
Date
Śaka 1059, 63rd year, Siṁha, ba. 14, Wednesday, Vyatīpāta.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Registers gift of money for a perpetual lamp in the temple of Karañjīśvara at Ippili, by a certain Rēvi-Nāyaka, son of Kommana-Nāyaka and Eṟakama-Nāyakuṟālu.

Mentions Yurujām.

VIZAGAPATAM DISTRICT


VIRAVALLI TALUK


ARIE/1929-1930/B/1929-30/5 (page 5)
Placement
Juttada.--On a slab built into the floor in front of the Veṅkaṭēś-vara temple in the village.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 123*, Paushya, ba. ashṭamī, Fri-day, Uttarāyaṇa.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Fragmentary. Seems to register grant of land for half a lamp to the temple of Janārdana. Another fragment in later characters appears to record gift of money and men-tions Gaṅgasāni.
ARIE/1929-1930/B/1929-30/6 (page 5)
Placement
On a stone lying in front of the same temple.
Dynasty
Matsya
King
Mahāmaṇḍālēśvara Bhīmarāja
Date
3rd year, Uttarā-yaṇa-saṅkrānti, Thursday.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Registers grant of land by Bhīmi-Seṭṭi, son of Prōli-Seṭṭi of Sauḍāvuram, for a perpetual lamp in the temple of the goddess Vindhyavāsinī of Duttāḍa.
ARIE/1929-1930/B/1929-30/7 (page 5)
Placement
On a broken pillar lying behind the same temple.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Vallabharāja
Date
Śaka 1385, Svabhā-nu, Jyēshṭha, pūrṇimā, Thurs-day.
Language
Sanskṛit in Telugu
Remarks
Records performance of an Agnishṭōma sacrifice by the king on the bank of the Dantā.

WEST GODAVARI DISTRICT


TANUKU TALUK


ARIE/1929-1930/B/1929-30/14 (page 6)

Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
…
Language
Telugu
Remarks
States that 6 puṭṭi of land was the inam given to the Vaikhānasa Uddaṇḍarāyani Rāmānujasvāmi for conduct-ing the daily worship of the gods Gōpālasvāmin, Kēśava-rāya, Pallakēśava and Hanumān at Duvva, the expenses for other services being met by the villagers and by the local officials.

PALNAD TALUK


ARIE/1929-1930/B/1929-30/20 (page 6)
Placement
Cherlagudipadu.--On a slab set up in a field about three miles to the south-east of the village.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1477, Ānanda, Āshāḍha, śu. 11.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Damaged. Registers grant of land to a Brahman named Mārambhaṭṭa by the grandson of Kurumaddi Mallārā-yanigāru and son of Sēshādrinātha of the Vipparla-gōtra who bore several birudas.
ARIE/1929-1930/B/1929-30/21 (page 6)
Placement
Paluvayi.--On a slab set up near the Śiva temple in the village.
Dynasty
Kāhatīya
King
Gaṇapatidēva-Mahārāja
Date
Śaka 1177, Rāksha-sa, Kārttika, śu. 15, Thursday.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
States that, while Gaṅgayya-Sāhiṇi, the faithful subōrdi-nate of the king was ruling the earth, a certain Ullēpalli Bāchi-Reḍḍi renovated the temple of Kāḷēśvara at Pāla-vāya including the pinnacle and that Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Padumbāyi-Amma, who was pleased with it made a gift of land to the temple, for the merit of her father Ammadēva and her husband Lakshmīdēva.
ARIE/1929-1930/B/1929-30/22 (page 7)

Telugu

States that the image of Hanumān was set up and a grant of land for offerings to it was made by a certain Chidu-rele-Ayyaṅgāru, for the merit of his parents.

ARIE/1929-1930/B/1929-30/26 (page 7)
Placement
On a pillar set up in front of the same temple.
Dynasty
Kākatīya
King
Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Rudradēva-Mahārāja
Date
Śaka 1209, Sarvajit, Phālguṇa, śu. 8. Thursday.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Records construction of the prākāra, maṇḍapa, gōpura, the compound wall (kōṭa) and the Garuḍagambha in the temple of Gōpinātha by a certain Nalla-Gōpāladāsa, who calls himself a dependent of Śrī-Modaliṅgāru of the family of Vīra-Nārāyaṇadāsa, for the merit of the king. Records also gift of land, tolls and oil-mill by Dāḍi Rudradēva, the son of the king.
ARIE/1929-1930/B/1929-30/27 (page 7)
Placement
Pedda Garlapadu.--On a stone set up in front of the Sītārāmasvāmin temple in the village.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1766, Krōdhi, Vaiśākha, śu [1] 5.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
States that the temple of Sītārāmasvāmin at Peda-Gārlapāḍu which had been constructed by Gariapāṭi Śēshāchalam of Takkeḷḷapāḍu had fallen into disuse on account of the famine in the year Nandana and that his sons Lakshmī-nārāyaṇa and Subbayya reconstructed the temple, procured the old images, consecrated them and obtained some lands as inam in the villages of Būdavāḍa, Gōgulapāḍu and Peda-Gārlapāḍu in the Palnad taluk, for their daily worship.

Attur.--On the north wall of the central shrine in the Sōmanāthē-śvara temple in the village.
Dynasty
Chōḷa
King
Rājarāja Rāja[kēsari]varman alias Rāja-rājadēva.
Date
24th year
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Beginnings of lines built in. Begins with the introduction tirumakaLpOla, etc. Records gift of sheep by a lady of Kalkuṟichchi in Tiruvaḻudi-vaḷanāḍu to the temple of Sōmanāthadēva for a perpetual lamp. In continua-tion of this inscription is another record of the [27]th year of the same king recording gift of sheep by a Veḷḷāḷa of Marudūr in Māṉavīra-vaḷanāḍu.
ARIE/1929-1930/B/1929-30/387 (page 40)
Placement
On the same wall
Dynasty
Do.
King
Rājarājakēsarivarman alias Rājarājadēva
Date
28th year
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Begins with the same introduction. Registers sale of land by the ūravar of Varaṇḍivayal to a regiment of the king, who made a tax-free gift of it for the midday offerings to the image of Puṟambālai-Piḷḷaiyār Gaṇapatiyār in the temple of Sōmanāthadēva alias Ten-Tiruppūvaṇam-Uḍaiyār at Āṟṟūr Śēndamaṅgalam, a brahmadēya of Kuḍa-nāḍu, a subdivision of Rājarāja-maṇḍalam.

ARIE/1929-1930/B/1929-30/393 (page 40)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Chōḷa-Pāṇḍya.
King
Māṟavarman alias Vikrama-Chōḷa-Pāṇḍya-dēva
Date
25th year
Language
Tamil
Remarks
States that the Śivabrāhmaṇas belonging to the aganāḻigai of the temple of Sōmanāthadēva at Āṟṟūr in Rājādhirāja-chaturvēdimaṅgalam, a brahmadēya in Kuḍa-nāḍu, a subdivision of Uttamachōḷa-vaḷanāḍu, a district of Rājarāja-Paṇḍināḍu, agreed to provide on every amāvāsyā day special offerings to the deity and to feed 15 Śivabrāhmaṇas in the temple, with the produce of the land endowed by a certain Kaṇḍaṉ Aiyaṉār alias Nṛipaśikhāmaṇi-Mūvēndavēḷār of Maṅgalakkāl who purchased it from the assembly of Rājādhirāja-chatur-vēdimaṅgalam. Mentions the measure called Sōma-nāthaṉ-marakkāl.

ARIE/1929-1930/E/1929-30/90 (page 71)
Placement
Slab standing near the Mallikārjuna temple.
Dynasty
Western Chāḷukya.
King
Tribhuvanamalladēva, ‘ruling from the rājadhānī Kalyāṇapura’
Date
Chāḷukya-Vikrama year 20, Yuva, Pushya, ba. [11], Monday, Uttarā-yaṇa-saṅkrānti.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
States that the crown-prince (yuvarāja) Mallikarjunadēva, who was governing the Tardavāḍi Thousand district, requested by his subordinate, the great general Bhīvaṇ-ayya, gave 100 mattar of land to the temple of the goddess Sarasvatī, into the hands of Chandraśēkhara-Paṇḍita, the disciple of Śāntarāśi-Paṇḍita, the āchārya of the maṭha of the temple of Svayaṁbhu Dakshiṇa-Sōmanāthadēva at Herbāḷ. Mentions Siriṁalaṁge.

ARIE/1929-1930/E/1929-30/96 (page 71)
Placement
Muttigi.--Slab built into the front wall (left side) of the Saṅgamēśvara temple.
Dynasty
Western Chāḷukya.
King
Pratapachakravarti Jagadēkamalladēva, ‘ruling from Kalyāṇapura’.
Date
10th year, Prabhava, Chaitra, ba 5, Monday, Vishu-saṅkrānti, Vyatī-pāta.
Language
Kannaḍa (prose & verse)
Remarks
Gives the genealogy of the Western Chāḷukyas from king Tailapa downwards and praises the king's subordinate, General Barmana, and a learned Brahman named Mādhavadēva and his son Śivarāja-chamūpa who built a trikūḷa temple at Muttage and at Vijayāpura. Records the gift, by the king, of the village of Nāgavāḍa, in Hebbāḷu Twelve, to the god Śivaliṅga at the agrāhara of Muttage situated in Muttage. Thirty in Tardavāḍi Thousand. Gives in detail the spiritual heirarchy of Lakuḷēśvara who actually received the gift. Records also the subsequent grant of certain taxes (baṇṇigadeṟe) by Hergaḍe Bammarasa, an officer under Daṇḍanātha Mailāra who was, as a subordinate of Bijjaḷadēva, governing the Tardavāḍi-nāḍu. Certain seṭṭis also made gifts of money to the temple of Śivaliṅga while the Mahājanas of the village gave some land to it.

Pārthiva, Āshāḍha, ba. 10, Thursday, Dakshiṇāyana-saṅkrānti.
Language
Kannaḍa

Registers the remission of the baṇṇigadeṟe tax on the garden of the same temple, by [Ha]mmarasa-Daṇḍanāyaka, the Aāhikari of Taddavāḍi Thousand and the several karaṇas as a paramēśvaradatti. ARIE/1929-1930/E/1929-30/114 (page 73)
Placement
Salvadigi.--Stone standing near the Hanumān temple.
Dynasty
Yādava
King
Prauḍhapratāpachakravarti Kaṁnhara-dēva.
Date
Śaka 1174, Virō-dhakṛit, Śrāvaṇa, śu. paurṇamī, Sunday, eclipse, saṅkrānti, Vyatī-pāta.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records the gifts of lands, oil, etc., made by Sīripayya, the son of Hariyanṇa of Hagaraṭṭage, who belonged to the Vā[ji]-vaṁśa and was the Śrīkaraṇa of the Mahāpra-dhāna Rāyadaṇḍādhiśa Sarvādhikāri, Chauḍi-Śeṭṭi who was governing over the Two [Beḷu ?]valas, Banavāsi-Pāṇḍyanāḍu, Hānuṁ[gal-Pāṇḍināḍu], Tardavāḍi, etc., countries while the latter's maternal uncle Raṅgarasa was governing the villages of Sālavāḍige, Bāgavāḍi etc. The gift was made for the benefit of the temple of Gōpāladēva and of the sixteen Mahājanas attached to the deity. Records also gifts of lands made to the temples of Lakshmaṇēśvaradēva and Bhāskaradēva.
ARIE/1929-1930/E/1929-30/115 (page 73)
Placement
Broken slab standing near the entrance to the Masjid.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
…
Language
Kannaḍa (verse)
Remarks
This is a composite record registering several facts and gifts. Praises king Śubhatuṅgavallabha born in the Rāshṭrakūṭa line, and Kannara and Akālavarsha, which were respectively the name and surname of Kṛishṇa II, who is also called Kṛishṇarāja in the inscription. States that his subordinate Horeyama-Sāmanta built a temple of Śiva at Sālavaḍige and that king Śubhatuṅga granted some land to it. Subsequently, when this temple fell into ruin a Śivayati named Mūṟudēvimuni renovated it and consecrated in it the two deities of Siddhēśvara and Pāpavināśadēva, to which land was given in the time of king Jagadēkamalla of the Chālukya line descended from king Nūrmaḍi-Tailapa, by Chikabbe, the daughter of a certain Mūliga Mākamayya. Gifts made by the four chief Prabhus or Ūroḍeyas of Sāḷavāḍige who belonged to the Ātrēya-gōtra and Vāji-vaṁśa, by the residents of the village and by the Three-Hundred Paṭṭasaligas are also recorded.

NORTH KANARA DISTRICT


HONAWAR TALUK


ARIE/1929-1930/E/1929-30/117 (page 74)
Placement
Bailur.--Slab standing near the Haslara huts.
Dynasty
Vijaya-nagara.
King
Virapratāpa Dēvarāya-Mahārāya
Date
Śaka 1356, Pra-mādi, Kārtika, ba. 10, ....
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records the gifts of lands, etc. made by Adhikāri Saṇṇu-Nāyaru and the several people of Bailūr, to a certain Nārāyaṇa-Bhaṭṭa for expounding the Purāṇas daily in the temple of Maḍakēśvara, and also the gifts made to the same donee by Surēśvara-Śrīpāda and the several people, for expounding the Purāṇas on the 30 days of the month of Śrāvaṇa in the maṭha of the Śrīpāda. The Mahāpradhāna Purushōttamadēva-Oḍeya was then ruling over the Tuḷu-rājya from the capital at Bārakūru.

Kumta.--Slab standing in a field.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
[Śaka 128]2, Vikāri, ...., Wednesday, Anūrādhā.
Language
Sanskṛit in Nāgarī & Kannaḍa
Remarks
Much damaged and mutilated.
